00:00:02
Tags: get_pi_token staging
Execution Time : 00:00:00
  • Given that a user needs to invoke "Get Staging PI Token"

    API Endpoint is:
    https://int-piapi-internal.stg-openclass.com/tokens

    HTTP Method is: POST

Execution Time : 00:00:00
  • And the user set the request payload as follows <file:/resources/payloads/login.txt>

    /resources/payloads/login.txt

    × 
    {
 "userName": "osanda12",
 "password": "Password1"
}

    The JSON request body that you are going to use for the API is:
    {
    “userName”: “osanda12”,
    “password”: “Password1”
    }
